  <span id="freeText16664693019749910197" style="display:none"><b>. : ☾⋆ — 1.5 ★</b><br /><br /><b>[SHARP INHALE] I’M FREEEEEEEEEEEEEEEE</b><br /><br />i never have to think about this series again. i know that sounds harsh but these books have brought me so much unnecessary anger and frustration that it’s truly a relief to finally FINALLY be done with the series once and for all. i can finally put these books down and be DONE with the characters and the story and v*ctoria av*yard’s nasty ass personality<br /><br />i actually didn’t completely hate this book (which was a very pleasant surprise!! i’m not gonna lie!!) but it was still uselessly long and very poorly plotted out and the final battle + the end was so UNDERWHELMING i genuinely wanted to claw my eyes out. like!!!!!!! @v*ctoria DID I REALLY JUST GO THROUGH 650 PAGES FOR THAT?????????????? i’m not gonna go into much detail about that since it’s very clearly a spoiler. however i WILL MOST DEFINITELY TALK ABOUT EVERYTHING ELSE THAT I DIDN’T LIKE<br /><br /><b>● unrestrained pining: </b>mare and cal spend the first 40% of the book going off about how they CAN’T be with each other despite the fact that they’re ~~ so in love ~~ because???/?????? because cal????????? is gonna be king of norta??????? BITCH THOSE ARE NOT EXCLUSIVE TO EACH OTHER THEY DON’T MATCH UP AT ALL!!!!! like being honest for a second cal and mare don’t need to be married to be together???? they don’t even have to make it public????? EVEN IF CAL MARRIES SOMEONE ELSE (EVANGELINE), MARE CAN STILL BE HIS LOVER?????? JUST AS ELANE IS EVANGELINE’S LOVER DESPITE THE FACT THAT SHE’S GONNA MARRY CAL?????????????? the worst part about this is that evangeline, in canon, in text, brings up this idea and she’s like “hey like u can be lovers lmao i don’t care i’m a lesbian i’m gonna hang out over here with my lesbian lover” and mare is like “I CAN’T BE WITH CAL HE CHOSE THE CROWN OVER ME :(” god i’m so fucking angry i don't even like mare and cal together but this was just so beyond STUPID<br /><br /><b>● strategizing/war stuff: </b> this book was trying way too hard to be the hunger games with all the surprise attacks and battles between the countries ON THAT NOTE when the FUCK did so many countries show up in this universe????? and why doesn’t the book have a map????? v*ctoria i’m a tired college student and i can’t keep up with all these useless countries. anyway the battle scenes didn’t make sense at all, and i feel like v*ctoria had all these sequences perfectly played out in her head but when it came down to writing them she kinda got a little excited and forgot to put some stuff in because spatially i could not for the life of me make sense of what was going on <br /><br /><b>● iris + the lakelands: </b>USELESSSSSSSSSSSS. DIDN’T DO ANYTHING. WASN’T EVEN ON THE EPILOGUE BECAUSE V*CTORIA HERSELF DIDN’T CARE. NEXT. <br /><br /><b>● cal and maven: </b><br /><br /><i> “I swear, these Calore brothers are trying to out-idiot each other.” </i><br /><br />this is an actual quote from the actual book and truer words have never been spoken, god bless. even though i love maven with every piece of my heart, he did some dumb shit in this book. cal also did some dumb shit. mostly cal did dumb shit. this boy can’t be king even if his life depended on it??? he’s awful at politics???? and no offense but maven in particular felt really out of character to me in the scenes where politics were involved because he just??? sucked??? when he was otherwise brilliant in the previous books???? why did u do my boy like that v*ctoria. why. i’m also extremely mad that we didn’t get the redemption arc we deserved because no OFFENSE but maven had the potential to become a new warner from shatter me and yet here we are :(<br /><br /><b>● zero character development: </b> THIS BOOK WAS ALMOST 700 PAGES LONG V*CTORIA WHYYYYYYYYYYYYYYYY<br /><br />anyway i had zero hopes for this book and was still somehow disappointed even though i did like some parts of it lmao bye bitch you best believe i’m never reading anything by v*ctoria av*yard ever again!!!!!!!!!!!</span>

<div id="review_2282390231" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2282390231" />
    <a title="Alexander Hamilton" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/62795872-alexander-hamilton"><img alt="Alexander Hamilton" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1501195593p2/62795872.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2282390231?book_show_action=true">May 26, 2018</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Alexander Hamilton" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Alexander Hamilton" href="/user/show/62795872-alexander-hamilton">Alexander Hamilton</a>
      </span>

        rated it

<div id="review_1713268265" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1713268265" />
    <a title="Cindy ✩☽♔" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3222333-cindy"><img alt="Cindy ✩☽♔" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1605643833p2/3222333.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1713268265?book_show_action=true">Jul 23, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Cindy ✩☽♔" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Cindy ✩☽♔" href="/user/show/3222333-cindy">Cindy ✩☽♔</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3222333-cindy?shelf=fantasy">fantasy</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1713268265" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2434222743582605790"><b> Rise. And rise alone. </b> <br/><br/>Red Queen was the book that fully immersed me into the YA book world. Taking me from an occasional reader to a full-on bookaholic. For that, it will always have a special place in my heart. <br/><br/>Let's start with saying this book is monstrous in size compared to its predecessors. But fortunately, it never feels excessive and it doesn't needlessly drag on. This series has been a tumultuous journey and this book is no exception. <br/><br/><b>Characters</b><br/><u>Mare</u> <br/><a href='http://tinypic.com?ref=2eatsep' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1509061821ra/24288521.gif' alt='Image and video hosting by TinyPic' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/>She did it. Mare did exactly wha</span>
  <span id="freeText2434222743582605790" style="display:none"><b> Rise. And rise alone. </b> <br><br>Red Queen was the book that fully immersed me into the YA book world. Taking me from an occasional reader to a full-on bookaholic. For that, it will always have a special place in my heart. <br><br>Let's start with saying this book is monstrous in size compared to its predecessors. But fortunately, it never feels excessive and it doesn't needlessly drag on. This series has been a tumultuous journey and this book is no exception. <br><br><b>Characters</b><br><u>Mare</u> <br><a href="http://tinypic.com?ref=2eatsep" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1509061821ra/24288521.gif" alt="Image and video hosting by TinyPic" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br>She did it. Mare did exactly what I had hoped she'd do. She chose the revolution. Though I do question some of her other choices later in the book she continually stood firm when it mattered. <br><br><u>Cal</u> <br>How I felt about Cal most of the book<br><a href="http://tinypic.com?ref=n6ck15" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1526670500ra/25563164.gif" alt="Image and video hosting by TinyPic" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br>It's important to note, Cal is not a bad person. He is just so rooted in his beliefs, and the way for his people that he is unable to fully embrace the change, the revolution, his country needs to undergo. He does ultimately do the right thing though so I guess I have to give him some credit for that. But I can't escape that linger feeling that if the tides had been in his favor he would've ridden that wave and stayed the course. <br><br><u>Maven</u> <br><a href="http://tinypic.com?ref=f4h92r" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1521474766ra/25238663.gif" alt="Image and video hosting by TinyPic" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br>I know it’s completely irrational, but I still had this desperate hope that somehow, someway Maven would redeem himself. Show some sliver of goodness, of the person he could’ve been if his mind hadn’t been poisoned. But instead, Ms. Aveyard just doubles down on Maven's villainy. <br><br>Honestly, it almost felt like a bit of a regression in terms of his character development. In King's Cage, we had Mare seeing Maven as a broken young man. A victim of mind manipulation, with which he had no say, who felt completely and utterly alone. And honestly, it made me feel for him. He was a monster, but not one of his own making. However, in this book, despite the addition of Maven's POV, rather than further establish or understand his brokenness. We are lead to believe, at least in some instances, that Maven chooses to remain this monster? It doesn't make sense. If Elara mind manipulation is so complete and irrevocable there shouldn't be a choice. <br><br><u>Evangeline</u> <br>Never thought I'd say it but...<br><a href="http://tinypic.com?ref=211tohc" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1526670382ra/25563161.gif" alt="Image and video hosting by TinyPic" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br>Honestly, it's amazing what some perspective can do for a character. I never cared for Evangeline in the first book, but as the series went on her actually become one of my favorite characters. Like most of the others, she was a product of her environment. Being able to see things from her point of view gave me a much greater appreciation of her and everything she has been through. <br><br><u>Iris</u> <br><a href="http://tinypic.com?ref=30bfuqc" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1509382625ra/24315100.gif" alt="Image and video hosting by TinyPic" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br>What can I say, she's the enemy. So hating her is a given. <br><br><b>Relationships</b><br><u>Mare &amp; Cal</u><br>I think a lot of people will be disappointed, but personally <br><a href="http://tinypic.com?ref=rkd4c4" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1526669766ra/25563152.gif" alt="Image and video hosting by TinyPic" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><u>Maven &amp; Mare</u><br>This relationship has always been my favorite. From friends, to love interests, to enemies they always had the most interesting dynamic. But I don't think I alone in saying that I found their end disappointing. <br><br><u>Cal &amp; Maven</u> <br>We finally got Cal and Maven's perspectives in this book, yet we did not get a single brother only discussion or confrontation? I call BS! Ugh...such a missed opportunity. <br><a href="http://tinypic.com?ref=24489e1" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1526669723ra/25563149.gif" alt="Image and video hosting by TinyPic" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><u>Mare &amp; Evangeline</u> <br>This friendship, or at least cease-fire, was unexpected but rather delightful. Two strong women who have been deeply shaped by their circumstances, coming together against all odds and developing an understanding and appreciation of each other. I'm here for it!<br><br><u>Cal &amp; Evangeline</u> <br>These two have been thrown together time and time again. Two high houses of Norta looking strengthen their hold on the nation with a political marriage. Neither of them ever wanted the other. It was simply what was expected of them by their families. But by books end, I think they did have a mutual respect for one another and how similar they really were. <br><br>The ending was not what I expected. In a way, it's what I thought I wanted. And in many ways, it is a fitting end. But it also doesn't truly feel like an ending? It feels like the sort of end that actually marks a beginning. As though this story is not actually over. Does that make sense?</span>
  <a data-text-id="2434222743582605790" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <span id="freeText14212647421562581583" style="display:none">1* for the Maven chapters<br>My black little ♥is broken 😢<br><br>So my dear friends we have come to the end of a very boring era. <br>Look out for spoilers ahead. Gonna tag it<br> <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ <br>I am gonna say that if you have hope for Maven then dont bother to read this book because it will only hurt you and leave you depressed.<br>The chapters from his view was the saddest. We got a close up look at the raw pain he felt. <br><br>So guys Victoria Aveyard led us to think that book 3 actually had a reason. She gave us hope that Maven could actually be fixed. This book was so lazy for fixing Maven. They didnt even try. They just killed him at the end. How pathetic. I hate it sm. <br><br>Mare is annoying as f***<br>They characters were still so bland and Evangeline felt like the only saving grace besides Maven. <br>What i am angry abt is that the author gave Maven so many layers and showed us a broken, sad and painful side of him leading us to think that he could be redeemed in some way. She even made Mare friggin Barrow have very mixed feelings abt him throughout the series leading me to believe that he was not just your common villian. That he could be saved. After kings cage i taught Mare had seen a side of Maven that no one else had and it was not all for nothing.<br><br>And to make it even worse she was the one to kill him. Like why make me see this hurt side of Maven if you are just gonna kill him like a common murder like every other book? So much potential wasted. <br>And this book just felt bland and the plot felt like glass sword. So darn boring. Maybe it could have been a duology but instead the author made me fall for the villian along with many other readers just to snatch that hope. As a ya book authors should try to portray that people can change nd ppl will say that not everyone changes but Mare spent so much time thinking about and obsessing over Maven that i would have taught she would have accomplished something positive. But she was her barbaric ole self to scared to show her true self hiding like a scared little gurl. I am never gonna read another va book. She played with my emotions well and i am so done. But then again i should not feel disappointed because as others say this is just recycled storylines and nothing original. Doe she even realise that by making us love Maven and killing him would only lead to us trusting her future books even less? Why tho?<br><br>Maven was the only reason this series even seemed a bit remotely interesting to me and deep down i knew it would not be happily ever after because only some very talented authors can turn around their stories like that but stupid me still had hope. There are tons of alternatives for him instead of death. <br><br>Surprisingly i did not hate Cal. He was just kinda like wallpaper. <br>I actually liked Evangeline and i didnt mind reading from her point which is shocking. <br>As always i found the other characters boring and predictable with Maven being the only one with actual layers to his character. I would have liked to know more about the boy he liked who died though but right now i am just so upset over everything. <br><br>And if you were wondering how it ended then Mare kills Maven and she leaves and tells Cal that they need time to heal and not to wait for her. So she ends up with none of them. This one of the only satisfying thing however Cal shippers may be disappointed. <br> <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br>End of rant for now. Maybe tomorrow i will have more taughts. <br><br>Such a big let down. Come to think of it i never like dumbass mare. She just caused more problems in the series. I can now c y so many ppl hate her. The only decent thing she actually did was at the very end of the book. <br> <br>I am not saying to not read the book but this is just my taughts and in conclusion i wasted so much time and money for this book. <br><br>Before reading<br>If you have read my previous review fthen you will know that the last book wasn't the best for me. Anyway never fear! Fori still have a little faith thus far and anything is possible. So for my Maven ship:<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1571265843ra/28304995.gif" width="300" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Even if it sinks to the bottom of the ocean<br><br>And to Victoria<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1492303219ra/22503871.gif" width="300" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br> Sorry for all the Pirates of the Caribbean but I couldn't help it ;)<br><br>Update<br><i>War Storm ????<i> Hmmmm<br><br>I don't think its the best. <span id="freeTextContainer1161594788048621613">well, folks. its happened. another series has come and gone. and yet again im feeling relatively unimpressed about the whole experience. maybe its the fact that i turned 27 today and im just getting too old and cynical for this type of book or maybe the book/story/writing/plot is to blame. why not both?! my old age aside, this left me feeling very… unsatisfied. i appreciate the effort that went into telling/writing this story, but i felt like this often dragged (which was frustrating because of </span>
  <span id="freeText1161594788048621613" style="display:none">well, folks. its happened. another series has come and gone. and yet again im feeling relatively unimpressed about the whole experience. maybe its the fact that i turned 27 today and im just getting too old and cynical for this type of book or maybe the book/story/writing/plot is to blame. why not both?! my old age aside, this left me feeling very… unsatisfied. i appreciate the effort that went into telling/writing this story, but i felt like this often dragged (which was frustrating because of its length), i wish i would have gotten more cal and maven (did we really even need iris’ perspective??), and i just didnt feel like this was the ending this series (or cal) deserved. to me, this book definitely focused on quantity over quality, which is a shame. but i guess it is what it is and im finally free of this at last. <br /><br /><b>
  <i>3.5 stars</i>

<div id="review_1549621439" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1549621439" />
    <a title="♥ℂĦℝΪՖƬΪℕÅ" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/52207144"><img alt="♥ℂĦℝΪՖƬΪℕÅ" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1568965358p2/52207144.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1549621439?book_show_action=true">Jul 06, 2018</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="♥ℂĦℝΪՖƬΪℕÅ" class="user" itemprop="url" name="♥ℂĦℝΪՖƬΪℕÅ" href="/user/show/52207144">♥ℂĦℝΪՖƬΪℕÅ</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Audiobook 9780062841704" href="/book/show/35958924-war-storm">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/52207144?shelf=fantasy">fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/52207144?shelf=romance">romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/52207144?shelf=dystopia-and-utopian">dystopia-and-utopian</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/52207144?shelf=magic">magic</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/52207144?shelf=2018-reading-challenge">2018-reading-challenge</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/52207144?shelf=young-adult">young-adult</a>
          </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1549621439" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17181435220074624187"><u>3 Rise With The Dawn ★'s</u> <br/><br/>What the hell? Seriously? That's it? <b>War Storm</b> is the FINAL book in the <i>Red Queen</i> series and I must say I'm a bit disappointed and a little upset right now. I thought it started out strong, then about the midpoint, it all just fell short. I was really excited for this, I mean it's been one of my favorite series and this is what I get? I can't freaking believe this is how Victoria Aveyard chose to end it and it definitely didn't need to be such a long book but what are yo</span>
  <span id="freeText17181435220074624187" style="display:none"><u>3 Rise With The Dawn ★'s</u> <br><br>What the hell? Seriously? That's it? <b>War Storm</b> is the FINAL book in the <i>Red Queen</i> series and I must say I'm a bit disappointed and a little upset right now. I thought it started out strong, then about the midpoint, it all just fell short. I was really excited for this, I mean it's been one of my favorite series and this is what I get? I can't freaking believe this is how Victoria Aveyard chose to end it and it definitely didn't need to be such a long book but what are you gonna do ¯\_(ツ)_/¯? It was slow and boring and anytime there was a "battle" I felt that it was over so quickly and way too easily won. Also, I was really disappointed in Maven's POV. It didn't really add anything to the story. I love the cover and the title but sadly whats inside didn't live up! I will say chapter <i>Thirty</i> and <i> Thirty-Two made my heart hurt. I was really expecting a lot more! Ugh... We didn't even get to see an HEA♥ 😭😭! <br><br><b>#teamCal Forever!!</b><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1530936759ra/25935803.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1406622686i/10574845._SX540_.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><i>“Love can be exploited, I guess, used to manipulate. It's leverage. But I would never call loving someone else a weakness. I think living without love at all, any kind of love, is weakness. And the worst kind of darkness.”</i><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1530936759i/25935802._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></i></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer834970506514310773">What do I do with my life now?! <br/><br/>Sorry. That did't sound right. Let me try again.<br/><br/>WHAT DO I DO WITH MY LIFE NOW ARRRGHHHHH!!!!!! (Click this tag to hear more screaming noises which accurately describe my feelings: <a class='jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction'>(view spoiler)</a><span class='spoilerContainer' style='display: none'>[AHHHHHHHHHHHHHHHHHhhhhhh.... ATJFJFADUFYIGFAIOPPWUIRADGRJHvfsdkasjbgfryGsuyrgseurygAygKUykGYKsygksyufgrGYayugragAVgasdfgghjjklASDFGHJKL!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!! *pterodactyl screeches* *dying cow noises* *suffocating goose* *mongolian throat singing* AWRSDJYRUEIWEI</span></span>
  <span id="freeText834970506514310773" style="display:none">What do I do with my life now?! <br /><br />Sorry. That did't sound right. Let me try again.<br /><br />WHAT DO I DO WITH MY LIFE NOW ARRRGHHHHH!!!!!! (Click this tag to hear more screaming noises which accurately describe my feelings: <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[AHHHHHHHHHHHHHHHHHhhhhhh.... ATJFJFADUFYIGFAIOPPWUIRADGRJHvfsdkasjbgfryGsuyrgseurygAygKUykGYKsygksyufgrGYayugragAVgasdfgghjjklASDFGHJKL!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!!! *pterodactyl screeches* *dying cow noises* *suffocating goose* *mongolian throat singing* AWRSDJYRUEIWEIQUWPPREKBMMVVVJAGEYGR *beluga whale* *dying pig sounds* *suffocating mongoose noises* *sound that an ant presumably makes when it drowns* NOOOOOOOOOOOOOOO (In the same tone of being distraught that Luke used in The Empire Strikes Back) *flailing hippopotamus* *general death noises* *Just me being a drama queen as I suffer emotional trauma at the hands of a paperback* AND MORE SCREECHING!!!)<br /><br />(That's probably the most coherent thinking you will get out of me TBH. It's definitely the most accurate...)<br /> <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>)<br /><br />I'm gonna do a spoiler free section because I am often the last to read new releases and know how frustrating it is to see just spoiler tags, but brace yourselves, for lots of ALLCAPS!!! (though I think I managed to restrain myself quite well right until the end if I'm honest here.)<br /><br />Okay. I love the series. Let me just start by saying that if you haven't yet read them, GO DO IT NOW YOU WILL NOT REGRET IT!<br /><br />I think that one of the many things War Storm did brilliantly was the pacing. I love all the other books in the series to pieces, but I will definitely admit that there were some parts in Glass Sword, and even a few in King's Cage, that dragged. This didn't bother me in the slightest, but REST ASSURED, War Storm pacing is PERFECTION THE WHOLE WAY!<br /><br />I can't really talk plot without spoilers, but it was super awesome and brilliant and WOW. It never ceases to amaze me how authors are so brilliant and can come up with so many fantastic ideas. I honestly do not think that there will be many people at all who are disappointed in the plot. It was really awesome.<br /><br />I think the characters are what will make or break this book for most people. But I'm pretty sure that no matter who you're rooting for (though I don't honestly understand why people care about anyone other than Cal, Mare, Cameron, Gisa or Evangeline) I think that there's something in there for you. Also, THERE WERE FIVE PERSPECTIVES AND THEY WERE DONE SO BEAUTIFULLY!!! Click if you don't mind finding out who they are: <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ The predictable Mare, the awesome Evangeline, the unexpected Iris, MY ABSOLUTE FAVE CINNAMON ROLL CAL, and ALSO MAVEN WHICH I WAS SO EXCITED ABOUT I ACTUALLY NEARLY SCREAMED WHEN I SAW IT AND THAT WAS A STROKE OF PURE BRILLIANCE!!!  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br />But yes. Generally, I think that overall you will all love it, but just... brace yourself. Just in case...<br /><br />Anyways. The spoilery bit starts now: <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Just want to start by saying that EVANGELINE TRYING TO GET CAL AND MAVEN BACK TOGETHER IS ACTUALLY MY FAVOURITE THING IN THE UNIVERSE I WANT TO THANK VICTORIA AVEYARD SO MUCH FOR WRITING THIS I WILL READ IT ON REPEAT. Chapters 16 &amp; 23 are some of my all time favourite pieces of literature in the universe, and I will be forever grateful that they have been written. <br /><br />Other than that I'm just going to give a general OH MY GOODNESS EVERYTHING WAS INCREDIBLE AND FANTASTIC AND I AM STILL REELING IT WAS SO GOOD!!! FARLEY WAS AN ALL ROUND LEGEND AND THE ACTION SCENES WERE SO WELL WRITTEN AND THE STAKES WERE HIGH AND EVERYTHING WAS AMAZING!!! Until we get to the epilogue...<br /><br />I met Victoria Aveyard in person a few weeks ago, and she said there would be closure. She didn't promise everyone would survive (though they basically did really. Maven was the only major loss in the book, which I didn't see coming. I actually faced a lot less emotional trauma than I expected...) or that it would be a happy ending, but she said that since it was the last book, there would be closure. AND I SINCERELY DISAGREE WITH THIS STATEMENT!!!<br /><br />As I sit here eating my leftover Thai food, I have so many questions. I would list them, but I don't know where to start and the list would be too long, and also, you probably already have them in your head. But seriously though, I just need another book. Here's to hoping that this: <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/39937558.Aveyard_Short_Story_Collection" title="Aveyard Short Story Collection by Victoria Aveyard" rel="nofollow noopener">Aveyard Short Story Collection</a> will answer all my questions, because I have SO MANY THAT I DON'T KNOW HOW THEY CAN EVER ALL BE ANSWERED!!<br /><br />But seriously though, WHY IS CAL NOT IMMEDIATELY BACK TOGETHER WITH MARE?! WHEN THEY WERE FIGHTING BEFORE THEY STILL WERE SO IN LOVE WITH EACH OTHER THOUGH THEY TRIED TO DENY IT AND EVERYBODY WAS INFURIATED BECAUSE THEY WERE JUST PRETENDING THEY DIDN'T CARE. AND THEIR EMBRACE ON THE BATTLEFIELD AS WELL! THAT SURELY SHOULD MEAN THAT THEY ARE STILL GOOD TOGETHER. AND I GET THAT CAL'S STILL UPSET ABOUT MAVEN BECAUSE I AM TOO! I'M STILL UPSET ABOUT STUFF THAT HAPPENED THREE BOOKS AGO OF WHAT HE DID. BUT CAL ADMITTED THAT MAVEN WAS LOST, HE WAS GOING TO KILL MAVEN HIMSELF UNTIL HE LOST HIS NERVE (which is completely understandable) BUT HE KNEW THAT MAVEN HAD TO DIE, AND HE KNEW THAT MARE WAS GOING TO DO IT, AND HE DIDN'T TRY TO STOP HER! WHY IS THIS SUCH A BIG OBSTACLE I JUST WANT THEM TO BE TOGETHER AND BE HAPPY AND I KNOW THEY HAVE STUFF TO WORK OUT BUT I WANT THEM TO WORK IT OUT TOGETHER, NOT SPEND TIME APART!!! (I'm only slightly obsessed...)<br /><br />I really think that Victoria Aveyard should take epilogue writing lessons, because the entire rest of her books are always perfection, and then she just writes an epilogue which will emotionally damage me forever.<br /> <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span></span>

<div id="review_2572111500" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2572111500" />
    <a title="Charlotte May" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/14002983-charlotte-may"><img alt="Charlotte May" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1596906925p2/14002983.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2572111500?book_show_action=true">Mar 13, 2019</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Charlotte May" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Charlotte May" href="/user/show/14002983-charlotte-may">Charlotte May</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14002983-charlotte-may?shelf=500-page-plus">500-page-plus</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14002983-charlotte-may?shelf=dystopia">dystopia</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14002983-charlotte-may?shelf=epic-fantasy">epic-fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14002983-charlotte-may?shelf=ya">ya</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14002983-charlotte-may?shelf=romance">romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14002983-charlotte-may?shelf=sisters">sisters</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2572111500" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12233378982772152685">3.5 ⭐️<br/><br/>Ok, so I can say with all honesty that this series does improve drastically. Victoria Aveyard’s writing and character development gets so much better!<br/><br/>When I read Glass Sword and King’s Cage, Mare was pissing me off so much I didn’t even want to continue with this series – especially considering the size of War Storm. However, I powered on through because I wanted to see how it would all end, and to be fair, I am glad I did.<br/><br/>War Storm has split POVs, which really helps lower Mare on the irri</span>
  <span id="freeText12233378982772152685" style="display:none">3.5 ⭐️<br /><br />Ok, so I can say with all honesty that this series does improve drastically. Victoria Aveyard’s writing and character development gets so much better!<br /><br />When I read Glass Sword and King’s Cage, Mare was pissing me off so much I didn’t even want to continue with this series – especially considering the size of War Storm. However, I powered on through because I wanted to see how it would all end, and to be fair, I am glad I did.<br /><br />War Storm has split POVs, which really helps lower Mare on the irritation scale. Along with Evangeline Samos, Iris Signet and also a couple of chapters from Cal’s and Maven’s perspective it made for a really interesting read. The 3 strong female protagonists were definitely great to read about and contrast with one another.<br /><br />Full of politics and double crossing. Everyone has an agenda, and even allies cannot trust one another. King Tiberias (Cal), his grandmother Anabel and his Uncle Julian have aligned themselves with the Scarlet Guard, those from Montfort (the land ruled by Premier Davidson where reds and silvers mix as equals), the newbloods and Cal’s betrothed – Evangeline and her family. Meanwhile Maven and the Signet family (aka the nymphs from the Lakelands) fight from the other side.<br /><br />There are many battles, to be honest I lost count a few times. I loved reading the different perspectives and seeing what each character wanted to get out of the war. I wanted to know what would happen to Maven in the end. I liked the ending <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ Mare murders Maven, and rightly so I think. But her and Cal still don’t get together in the end? I mean I’m not a romantic at all – but we just had four books of pining and then they don’t even get together? Like what? Cal needs to adjust to the fact that Mare killed Maven – even though we all know someone had to do it! At least Cal turned down his crown in order to work towards a world of equality, so that's something  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br />It’s been a long time coming, and I’m glad I read this series, but I’m also glad to be done with it. Goodbye Lightning Girl – I probably won’t miss you all that much.<br /><br /><br />************************<br /><br />So my copy of this has finally arrived in the library. Though I haven't read the first three since last Summer I cannot be bothered to reread them, so hopefully I'll remember stuff as I go....</span>
  <a data-text-id="12233378982772152685" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_1629827037" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1629827037" />
    <a title="AleJandra" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/25897549-alejandra"><img alt="AleJandra" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1488738602p2/25897549.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1629827037?book_show_action=true">May 05, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="AleJandra" class="user" itemprop="url" name="AleJandra" href="/user/show/25897549-alejandra">AleJandra</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/25897549-alejandra?shelf=fantasia">fantasia</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/25897549-alejandra?shelf=new-adult">new-adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/25897549-alejandra?shelf=distopicos">distopicos</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/25897549-alejandra?shelf=young-adult">young-adult</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1629827037" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8705261692783040916"><b>
  <u>4.5 <i>Shame and pride, sorrow and relief </i> STARS </u>
  <br/>
  <br/>
  <blockquote>
    <i>"The guns will quiet, the smoke will clear, and the soldiers, Red and Silver both, will come home."</i>
  </blockquote>
</b><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1527466724ra/25607078.gif' width='500' height='260' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Hay muchas cosas negativas que les puedo decir de este libro. Pero si ya han llegado a este punto de la serie, creo que ya no tiene caso mencionar todas aquellas críticas que ya discutimos con anterioridad. <br/><br/>Aquí la gran verdad de este libro, la razón por la que le estoy dando las 5 ESTRELLAS, es porque <b>Victoria Aveyard </b>de alguna man</span>
  <span id="freeText8705261692783040916" style="display:none"><b>
  <u>4.5 <i>Shame and pride, sorrow and relief </i> STARS </u>
  <br>
  <br>
  <blockquote>
    <i>"The guns will quiet, the smoke will clear, and the soldiers, Red and Silver both, will come home."</i>
  </blockquote>
</b><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1527466724ra/25607078.gif" width="500" height="260" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Hay muchas cosas negativas que les puedo decir de este libro. Pero si ya han llegado a este punto de la serie, creo que ya no tiene caso mencionar todas aquellas críticas que ya discutimos con anterioridad. <br><br>Aquí la gran verdad de este libro, la razón por la que le estoy dando las 5 ESTRELLAS, es porque <b>Victoria Aveyard </b>de alguna manera, logro hacerme leer su serie completa, a pesar de ser un género que no me gusta, con libros de más de 500 páginas, y con una historia llena de subidas y bajadas. Pero lo logro, que es más de lo que puedo decir de otras historias, que, aunque quizá sean mejor, nunca han mantenido mi interés.<br><br>Especialmente en este momento de mi vida en el que estoy tan metida en las novelas gráficas, que regresar a leer una novela me cuesta el doble de trabajo, así que si, solo por eso, War Storm se merece un aplauso de pie. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1527466724ra/25607079.gif" width="500" height="220" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Pero bueno, hemos llegados al final, es tiempo de decirle adiós a todos los personajes con los que hemos sobrevivido tanto por más de 3 años. Así que sin más vueltas:<br><br><b>Hablemos de War Storm<br>SPOILER ALERT<br><br><u>📚 Sinopsis Honesta:</u></b><br>El Reyno de Norta se enfrenta a una guerra civil, y guerra con sus imperios vecinos. Silvers y Reds tendrán que afrontar muertes, peleas, sufrimientos y difíciles decisiones. Esta es la historia de una REVOLUCION, NO UNA HISTORIA DE AMOR. Llena de batallas, enfrentamientos y manipulaciones. <br><br>Uno de los puntos fuertes de esta historia, que para mí la hizo diferente y sobresaliente a todas las demás, es que la historia tiene tantas tramas, que la relación amorosa de los protagonistas queda en segundo plano. Si la vemos obvio y juega un punto fuerte en la historia, pero no es el eje principal. <br><blockquote>
  <br>
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1527466724ra/25607080.gif" width="350" height="420" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</blockquote><br><br>Para mí el eje principal, es la revolución, los silver, reds y newblods, tratando de sobrevivir juntos. Ver como tratan de cambiar un sistema de gobierno completo, es muy interesante de ver. Los juegos de traiciones y alianzas entre las personas al poder, y que al final cada decisión se lleva acabo de forma calculada, y cada uno solo ve por si mismo, y por lo que creen que es correcto. <br><br><b>Hablemos de los personajes:<br><br>➦Mare</b><br>Mare no es un personaje que me fascine, pero si la respeto, desde el primer libro se ha mantenido fiel a sus convicciones, a pesar de amar a Cal y Maven, nunca ha dejado que sus sentimientos por ellos opaquen sus ideales y su búsqueda por la igualdad entre silvers y reds. Y así siguió su camino hasta el final, tomo malas decisiones, cometió errores, pero siempre siendo fiel a sí misma, como debe de ser, no pude pedir más para este personaje. Y si fui feliz con su final.<br><br><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>“He still hasn’t turned away from the crown, and I am still just as dedicated to my cause, if not more so. I can’t still be in love with a king, when everything I’m doing is to destroy his throne. Destroy all notions of kings and queens and the kingdoms at the mercy of their will.”</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1527466724ra/25607081.gif" width="500" height="260" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>➦Cal</b><br>Pobre Cal, le toco lo peor, sufrió sufrió sufrió. Tomo muy malas decisiones y tuvo que afrontar las consecuencias, pero lo entendí, y logre perdonarlo y no pude dejar de sentir lastima por su situación. Al igual que Mare, me gusto que sus sentimientos por ella no opacaron sus propios ideales. Al final el mismo tuvo que decidir a donde llevar a su país, y que tipo de gobernador quiere ser.<br><br><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>“When the storm breaks, I’ll be ready. I promise you that.” <br>Ready to fight. To lose. And probably die.”</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1527466724ra/25607082.gif" width="500" height="220" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>➦Iris</b><br>No me gustaron sus capítulos, y odie al personaje, poderosa pero aburrida como villana. Su traición fue lo mas obvio de la historia, se veía venir desde su primer capítulo. Lo mejor de ella, fue verla en batalla, que casi matara a Cal fue de lo mas intenso. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1527466724ra/25607083.gif" width="500" height="240" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>➦Evangeline</b><br>Al final fue el personaje que más evoluciono, y la única que logro su final feliz.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1527466724ra/25607084.gif" width="500" height="220" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>➦Maven</b><br>Oh mi Maven hermoso. Sus capítulos, aunque pocos fueron los más tristes. El chico perdido, roto y sin salvación. Todo el libro se la paso contra la esquina, sin salida, con todos en contra, hasta el mismo. No importante cuanto deseáramos verlo redimirse o ser feliz, el pobre ya había caído demasiado hondo en la locura, llore su desenlace, pero él no quería ser salvado.<br><br><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>“He has no loyalties, and no love in his heart. The boy who calls himself king is a shell, empty, a danger to everyone and everything.”</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1526704040ra/25564774.gif" width="500" height="240" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <u>Mis partes favoritas:</u>
</b><br><br>-	El enfrentamiento entre Cal e Iris fue épico.<br>-	Los <b>
  <i>“This is the last time” </i>
</b> de Mare y Cal.<br>-	El reencuentro entre Maven y Cal quería ver una pelea épica, pero su encuentro en la isla fue suficiente para romperme el corazón en cachitos.<br>-	Que Jhon reapareciera, esa platica con Mare lo fue todo.<br>-	Farley, toda ella es perfecta.<br>-	Y por supuesto el enfrentamiento entre Maven y Mare.<br><br>Como llore en este momento:<br><br><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>“I like the hair. We can still run. Together.”</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1527466724ra/25607086.gif" width="500" height="260" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1466107780ra/19440964.gif" width="500" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380430427ra/862973.gif" width="500" height="220" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><b> En conclusión:</b> Llegamos al final, para darnos cuenta de que realmente no hay final.<b>Nos dejan un final abierto,</b> se que a la mayoría les molesta este tipo de finales, a mí personalmente me encantan y son de mis favoritos.</span>
  <a data-text-id="8705261692783040916" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2802651906" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16662069141115578059"><b>War Storm (Red Queen, #4), Victoria Aveyard</b><br/><br/>Red Queen is a young adult fantasy novel written by American writer Victoria Aveyard. It was her first series and her first novel. It was published in February 2015. Its sequels are Glass Sword, King's Cage and War Storm. <br/><br/>War Storm is a strong finish to this series - the fight continues between the different factions of Reds and Silvers and Mare Barrow discovers new allies in this final volume. <br/><br/>تاریخ نخستین خوانش: روز چهارم ماه آگوست سال 2019میلادی<br/><br/>عنوان</span>
  <span id="freeText16662069141115578059" style="display:none"><b>War Storm (Red Queen, #4), Victoria Aveyard</b><br /><br />Red Queen is a young adult fantasy novel written by American writer Victoria Aveyard. It was her first series and her first novel. It was published in February 2015. Its sequels are Glass Sword, King's Cage and War Storm. <br /><br />War Storm is a strong finish to this series - the fight continues between the different factions of Reds and Silvers and Mare Barrow discovers new allies in this final volume. <br /><br />تاریخ نخستین خوانش: روز چهارم ماه آگوست سال 2019میلادی<br /><br />عنوان: طوفان جنگ: کتای چهارم سری ملکه سرخ؛ نویسنده: ویکتوریا آویارد؛ مترجم: فاطمه سعیدی، تهران، کتابسرای تندیس، 1397؛ در 712ص؛ فروست سری ملکه سرخ، کتاب چهارم؛ شابک 9786001823596؛ موضوع داستانهای نوجوانان از نویسندگان امریکایی - سده 21م<br /><br />کتاب «طوفان جنگ» درباره ی دو گروه از مردم با عنوان «خون سرخ»‌ها و «خون نقره ‌ای»‌ها است؛ «خون سرخ»‌ها که همان مردمان عادی و در واقع رعیت‌ها هستند، هیچ توانی به جز کار کردن ندارند؛ «خون نقره ‌ای»‌ها که خونشان رنگین است، افرادی با توانایی‌های ناباوانه هستند که در مسند قدرت قرار دارند، و بر «خون سرخ»‌ها فرمانروایی می‌کنند؛ هر جاییکه سخن از قدرت یگانه بیاید، به تبع آن سخن از فساد مفرط هم به میان می‌آید، ناعدالتی و ظلم «خون نقره ‌ای‌ها» بر مردمان عادی بیداد می‌کند؛ اما در این بین یک رویداد عجیب رخ می‌دهد؛ آن هم این که دختری هفده‌ ساله به نام «ماری بارو» که از «خون سرخ‌ها»ست، دارای توانایی (کنترل آذرخش) است، که تنها «خون نقره ‌ای»‌ها می‌توانند، چنان توانی داشته باشند؛ حال که «خون نقره ‌ای»‌ها متوجه آن امر می‌شوند، او را به قصر نقره ‌ای آورده، و به گونه ‌ای نمایش می‌دهند، که گویی او یکی از شاهزادگان گم شده بوده که تازه پیدا شده است، و تصمیم می‌گیرند او با یکی از پرنس‌های «خون نقره‌ ای» ازدواج کند؛ «ماری بارو» پا در قصری گذاشته که در شرایط عادی نیز، جای خطرناکی برای اوست، به گروهی مخفی به نام «گارد سرخ» می‌پیوندد؛ این گروه تصمیم بر سرنگونی حکومت بیداد «خون نقره‌ای»‌ها دارند<br /><br />در این رمان که کتاب پایانی از این سری چهار جلدی است، خوانشگران دیگر با «ماری» ساده و بی‌تجربه مواجه نیستند، بلکه با یک دختر توانمند و جسور، که دشواری‌ها و لحظات هولناکی را پشت سر گذاشته، رودررو هستند؛ دختری که باور دارد، باید قوی به نظر بیاید، حتی اگر آنگونه نباشد! در واقع در این جلد خوانشگر با شخصیتی روبرو می‌شود، که طعم تلخ خیانت از سوی «کال» را چشیده، کسیکه «ماری» به او علاقمند بوده است؛ دختری که به دنبال انتقام است، و تنها سرنگونی پادشاهی «نورتا» را، در سر دارد؛ ولی در اینراه «ماری» باید، دوباره در کنار پسریکه به او خیانت کرده، و دل او را شکسته، قرار بگیرد، تا بتواند نقشه ‌های خود را عملی کند؛ اما آیا او در این راه همه چیز را پیش بینی کرده است؟ <br /><br />تاریخ بهنگام رسانی 04/08/1399هجری خورشیدی؛ ا. شربیانی</span>
  <a data-text-id="16662069141115578059" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_1954948574" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1954948574" />
    <a title="Jenny Han" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/61855216-jenny-han"><img alt="Jenny Han" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1479952946p2/61855216.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1954948574?book_show_action=true">Mar 28, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jenny Han" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jenny Han" href="/user/show/61855216-jenny-han">Jenny Han</a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1641532638?book_show_action=true">May 18, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Ayesha (The Fifth Marauder) " class="user" itemprop="url" name="Ayesha (The Fifth Marauder) " href="/user/show/55972693-ayesha-the-fifth-marauder">Ayesha (The Fifth Marauder) </a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/55972693-ayesha-the-fifth-marauder?shelf=dystopia">dystopia</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1641532638" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11008426437501955077"><b>How did we go from <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/22328546.Red_Queen__Red_Queen___1_' title='Red Queen (Red Queen, #1) by Victoria Aveyard' rel='nofollow noopener'>Red Queen</a> to <i>this</i>??</b><br/><br/>When this book first got published, and many of my goodreads friends rated it quite low, a part of me hoped that it wasn't as bad as they said. See, I LOVED Red Queen. And I knew that the author was a good writer because <i>her battle scenes were amazingly written.</i><br/><br/>So this book for me was not just the end of a good series, but mainly <b>a chance at redemption after the disappointments that were Glass Sword and King's Cage.</b><br/><br/><u>Unfortunately, this ended up being an even </u></span>
  <span id="freeText11008426437501955077" style="display:none"><b>How did we go from <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/22328546.Red_Queen__Red_Queen___1_" title="Red Queen (Red Queen, #1) by Victoria Aveyard" rel="nofollow noopener">Red Queen</a> to <i>this</i>??</b><br /><br />When this book first got published, and many of my goodreads friends rated it quite low, a part of me hoped that it wasn't as bad as they said. See, I LOVED Red Queen. And I knew that the author was a good writer because <i>her battle scenes were amazingly written.</i><br /><br />So this book for me was not just the end of a good series, but mainly <b>a chance at redemption after the disappointments that were Glass Sword and King's Cage.</b><br /><br /><u>Unfortunately, this ended up being an even bigger let down.</u><br /><br />The multiple POVs became annoying as all the voices merged into one. Some of the best characters such as Evangeline, Iris and Cal were reduced to nothing more than whiny teenage brats who thought the world of themselves. Some were almost completely missing from the book such as Cameron and <s>Gale</s> -sorry- Kilorn.<br /><br /><b><u>The worst part was the conclusion.</u> At best it was confused and haphazard. At worst it was just nonsensical.</b> <br />After four dramatic books, the ending just seemed too forced and immature. <i>We don't even find out what happens to half the characters!</i><br /><br />Also <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[killing Maven and NOT EVEN SHOWING HIS DEATH SCENE??? UNCOOL!!! <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> That was almost as bad as building up to the big battle but everyone just talking it out instead of fighting in <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/1162543.Breaking_Dawn__Twilight___4_" title="Breaking Dawn (Twilight, #4) by Stephenie Meyer" rel="nofollow noopener">Breaking Dawn</a>.<br /><br />Kudos to Davidson, Farley and Maven; they were the only reason I bothered finishing this book. But even they weren't nearly as awesome as they were in the previous books. <b>
  <s>is there such a thing as REVERSE character development?</s>
</b><br /><br /><b>Pre read review:</b><br /><br />Me: orders War Storm.<br />Me: opens goodreads and sees all the hate reviews.<br />Me: slowly backs away.<br /><br />HEY at least the covers pretty ¯\_(ツ)_/¯</span>
  <a data-text-id="11008426437501955077" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

//<![CDATA[  

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('OhpdzsBllbsJ+qbWfHh3DNRaf5ShNFi/UYVKVtXO6F+kmU+rIr+OlPJlLNF4GGuLL2m1Uudavb2P38aEv7WRAg==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('jwCmSf1LdUQcD6Ece+duK6Pb6t1t/7+MmK3do0Y6dVURg7QsH5Fua+eQKxt/h3KsWOggGyuRWo5G91FxLEEMCA==')})
  }
//]]>
</script>
